<div id="review_912726791" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/912726791" />
    <a title="Brian O&#39;Hare" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25125581-brian-o-hare"><img alt="Brian O&#39;Hare" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442469396p2/25125581.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/912726791?book_show_action=true">Apr 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brian O&#39;Hare" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brian O&#39;Hare" href="/user/show/25125581-brian-o-hare">Brian O&#39;Hare</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer912726791" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6944481297775020922">Adds a whole new meaning to ‘reader empathy’!<br/><br/>Chaysing Deams by Jalpa Williby seizes the reader’s imagination from the first line and never lets go. Here is a writer with verve, imagination and a great story-telling talent. This is a romance story, yes, but romance with super helpings of mystery and creativity. It is an extraordinary tour de force that pushes the reader’s every emotional button. Such is Williby’s empathy with her main character’s heartaches and joys, that the reader in turn lives</span>
  <span id="freeText6944481297775020922" style="display:none">Adds a whole new meaning to ‘reader empathy’!<br /><br />Chaysing Deams by Jalpa Williby seizes the reader’s imagination from the first line and never lets go. Here is a writer with verve, imagination and a great story-telling talent. This is a romance story, yes, but romance with super helpings of mystery and creativity. It is an extraordinary tour de force that pushes the reader’s every emotional button. Such is Williby’s empathy with her main character’s heartaches and joys, that the reader in turn lives through every painful, every tortured, every joyous moment as though it were herself that was living this crazy whirlwind of a life.<br /><br />The principal character, Tessnia, or Tess, lives an apparently normal, if successful, life at school. But her nights are plagued by nightmares of someone being chased. Black clouds occasionally cross her vision during the day. She experiences almost mystical connections with Joe, with Chris, with Thunder and even with her dog, Gem. What is happening here? Jalpa Williby expertly weaves these inexplicable events into her story, whetting our appetite for explanation, teasing our expectations, forcing us to surge through the pages as we search hungrily for answers. <br /><br />Even from the very early stages we cannot help but try to formulate our own explanations. We wonder if Tess has some psychic or even supernatural powers. Has she? We wonder if there might be some kind of psychic connection between Joe and Chris. Is there? We even wonder if it might be possible that Joe and Chris are cosmic guardians designated to keep Tess safe from some other-worldly threat. Are they? This is how it is with Jalpa’s writing. The brain goes into high gear and the pages continue to fly…<br /><br />…and two destined souls meet, entwine and conjoin in the most lyrical of settings. Days pass in impossible bliss and suddenly the two are thrust into a harsh and furious chase, hurtling towards the story’s end, an end that is plausible, an end that is logical, an end that is, perhaps, inevitable. Oh, Chayse warns us so often that this is an ending we must expect. And it works….for Tessnia! But aaahh! – and what a sigh is there – my heart groans for Chayse.<br /><br />A stunning and wonderful book and a must read for lovers of the romance genre.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6944481297775020922" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_846758769" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/846758769" />
    <a title="Angie Martin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25063047-angie-martin"><img alt="Angie Martin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1408289422p2/25063047.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/846758769?book_show_action=true">Feb 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angie Martin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angie Martin" href="/user/show/25063047-angie-martin">Angie Martin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer846758769" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1895565456501319497">**I received a free copy of this book from the author in exchange for an honest and fair review**<br/><br/>If you love well-developed characters and a well-written romance novel, you will fully enjoy "Chaysing Dreams" by Jalpa Williby.<br/><br/>When I saw this book, the title instantly caught my attention. It's a very interesting title and the spelling of "chaysing" captured my curiosity. I just knew there was more of that to come and I wasn't disappointed. I'll have to be just a bit vague here so as not to give aw</span>
  <span id="freeText1895565456501319497" style="display:none">**I received a free copy of this book from the author in exchange for an honest and fair review**<br /><br />If you love well-developed characters and a well-written romance novel, you will fully enjoy "Chaysing Dreams" by Jalpa Williby.<br /><br />When I saw this book, the title instantly caught my attention. It's a very interesting title and the spelling of "chaysing" captured my curiosity. I just knew there was more of that to come and I wasn't disappointed. I'll have to be just a bit vague here so as not to give away any spoilers. The story itself is fantastic and the characters are great as well. Tess's character is very well developed, and so are the other secondary characters. There is a lot to Tess, and watching her character grow kept me very interested. And I have to say, I absolutely loved Jack and wish we had seen more of him in the book.<br /><br />The writing itself is outstanding, and that alone kept me turning the page. I have to say, though, I expected a little more suspense. At times it felt more like a straight romance novel. There were hints that something big would happen, but it took a long time to get there, and after half a book of these small hints, the suspense effect wore off to the point that I no longer expected something to happen. I hate even saying that because the book is wonderfully written with amazing characters and I literally couldn't stop turning the page once I started reading. I just wish there had been a bit more suspense throughout or that the action had started a bit sooner, since it is a romantic suspense novel and there were foreshadows of something big happening. BUT... This doesn't take away from the amazing quality of this book. Ms. Williby is a fantastic writer who deserves a lot of attention.<br /><br />Overall, I highly recommend this book to anyone who loves romance novels. The suspense does happen, but as long as you don't go into it expecting a big bang until the end and you'll be fine. The hook at the end did leave me wanting to read the next novel.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9744017524130708641"> Dreams. They come to us in the night taking us to places both familiar and foreign. They have the power to give us both delight and horror. Dreams free us and bind us all at once. Those of us who remember each and every nightly adventure see it as either a blessing or a curse.<br/><br/> For as long as Tess can remember she has had the same reoccurring nightmare. Despite her best efforts she can not shake the same scene from playing night after night. Each morning she awakes with the same feeling of anxie</span>
  <span id="freeText9744017524130708641" style="display:none"> Dreams. They come to us in the night taking us to places both familiar and foreign. They have the power to give us both delight and horror. Dreams free us and bind us all at once. Those of us who remember each and every nightly adventure see it as either a blessing or a curse.<br /><br /> For as long as Tess can remember she has had the same reoccurring nightmare. Despite her best efforts she can not shake the same scene from playing night after night. Each morning she awakes with the same feeling of anxiety and confussion. What does it all mean? Are they random images stuck on repeat or is there something more behind them?<br /><br /> The author begins Tess's journey as a teenager and develops her story over the course of a few years. It was great to see Tess grow from a typical teenage girl, to a hardworking college student, to a remarkable young woman. As the reader watches Tess grow up they get to witness key moments that will change her life forever. The 'normal' Tess thought she knew isn't so normal after all.<br /><br /> The author's writing was great! Her story development was spot on. She efficiently brought the characters to life. The dialogue among the characters was smooth and realistic. The one element of a novel I always take notice of is the authors use of words and their descriptions. Sometimes this can make or break a book for me. Jalpa nailed it for me with lines like, "The sky is the color of a robin's egg with tufts of small, white clouds on the horizon." Perfection! Also, I enjoyed the soundtrack of this novel. It brought the story to life and added a few new favorite songs to my iPod.<br /><br /> I am Jalpa Williby's newest fan and I hope after reading Chaysing Dreams you will be too. Look for Chaysing Dreams on Amazon.com and also be on the look out for the next book in this trilogy.<br /><br />Happy Reading!!<br /><a href="http://www.swooningoverbooks.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Swooning Over Books</a><br /><br /></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/753097345" />
    <a title="Kelli" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6284904-kelli"><img alt="Kelli" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378700051p2/6284904.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/753097345?book_show_action=true">Oct 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kelli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kelli" href="/user/show/6284904-kelli">Kelli</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6284904-kelli?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer753097345" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10666303684086377078">Unfortunately, I'm going to have to keep this review short and sweet. I can't really go into too much detail about this book due to the fact that I can't describe the storyline without revealing its mystery. This is just one if those stories that you'll have to experience for yourself. <br/><br/>I must admit, when I first began reading <i> Chaysing Dreams</i> I almost wanted to give up. However, something kept pushing me to give it a chance and see where it takes me. Luckily I listened to that pesky little voice</span>
  <span id="freeText10666303684086377078" style="display:none">Unfortunately, I'm going to have to keep this review short and sweet. I can't really go into too much detail about this book due to the fact that I can't describe the storyline without revealing its mystery. This is just one if those stories that you'll have to experience for yourself. <br /><br />I must admit, when I first began reading <i> Chaysing Dreams</i> I almost wanted to give up. However, something kept pushing me to give it a chance and see where it takes me. Luckily I listened to that pesky little voice because I was rewarded with a really interesting story in the end. I encourage readers to give this an honest chance because although it starts off slow and slightly annoying for lack of a better word, everything makes sense as the story develops.<br /><br />When I first met Tess, my first impression was that she was extremely naive and not someone I'd get along with in real life. She is 15 at the beginning of the story and her whole demeanor and perception of life is that of someone who has been fed with a silver spoon and has never had to endure any sort of suffering. Everything comes easily to her and she's never had to work at anything she has achieved in her short life. She has the picture perfect, loving family and has always excelled both academically and athletically. Her overly <i>happy</i> and positive attitude seemed too fake at first and I often found myself rolling my eyes while reading.<br /><br />However, like I said, for some strange reason I had to give her the benefit of the doubt and continued to follow her through her journey to adulthood. As the story progressed, I found myself glued to the story and wanting to find the answers behind the unique situations that came to light. I know this is really vague, but trust me when I say that it will all make sense in the end. The writing will eventually mature along with Tess and the characters are constantly being developed. Give it a chance, I really don't think you'll be disappointed.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10666303684086377078" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jada Ryker" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jada Ryker" href="/user/show/22078661-jada-ryker">Jada Ryker</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer796479184" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3957245105321022693">Tess' Story<br/><br/>In Chaysing Dreams, by Jalpa Williby, Tessnia Sanoby to have it all. She's beautiful, athletic, and intelligent. She has a great relationship with her loving parents. Her strong friendships include Kylie and Jack. She's earned her place on the high school varsity basketball team. She performs volunteer work with challenged children.<br/><br/>Below the glittering surface of her life is darkness. Tess has experienced freakishly realistic dreams, full of sight, sounds, and smells, for as long as s</span>
  <span id="freeText3957245105321022693" style="display:none">Tess' Story<br /><br />In Chaysing Dreams, by Jalpa Williby, Tessnia Sanoby to have it all. She's beautiful, athletic, and intelligent. She has a great relationship with her loving parents. Her strong friendships include Kylie and Jack. She's earned her place on the high school varsity basketball team. She performs volunteer work with challenged children.<br /><br />Below the glittering surface of her life is darkness. Tess has experienced freakishly realistic dreams, full of sight, sounds, and smells, for as long as she can remember. In her dreams, she is chased. Tess is terrified it's going to catch her. If it does, then she is doomed. To blur the line between the dreams and reality, a handsome and charismatic young man's piercing gray eyes appear in her dreams, urging her to safety. When Tess feels strong, unexpected connections to animals and experiences fear in the form of a black cloud in her waking hours, the darkness takes on a surreal shade.<br /><br />After graduating at the top of her high school class and starting college at Stanford, Tess is on the track team. A man is a baseball cap observes the practices. When he removes his cap and helps coach the track team, Tess is bowled over. Chris is drop dead gorgeous with wavy blonde hair, blue eyes, and an Australia accent that sends shivers down Tess' spine. A part of the school's elite military training program, Chris starts training Tess on the weekends.<br /><br />After suffering a shattering epiphany and profound loss, Tess reads a mysterious letter which changes her perspective on her entire life. She learns what Chayse really means. And her life takes an unexpected turn.<br /><br />Ms. Williby has woven an excellent story with wonderful characters. With her descriptions and talented prose, Ms. Williby allows the reader to live Tess' life with her. Experience Tess' triumphs, fears, grief, and adventures in Chaysing Dreams. I can't wait for the next installment in this thrilling trilogy.<br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3957245105321022693" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1081810366" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1081810366" />
    <a title="Kelly Pinella" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/35348269-kelly-pinella"><img alt="Kelly Pinella" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1411753709p2/35348269.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1081810366?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kelly Pinella" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kelly Pinella" href="/user/show/35348269-kelly-pinella">Kelly Pinella</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1081810366" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9372334501357890486">This story caught my interest right from the beginning. Tess is a smart, lovable high school student who has a passion for life. She is the only daughter of two respectable, kind, and loving parents. I became suspicious because Tess seemed to be too perfect in a perfect life. I knew that, sooner or later, something horrible was bound to happen, and I was not let down. When the "black cloud" enters into the story, I wanted to keep reading to find out what was causing this strange thing to happen.</span>
  <span id="freeText9372334501357890486" style="display:none">This story caught my interest right from the beginning. Tess is a smart, lovable high school student who has a passion for life. She is the only daughter of two respectable, kind, and loving parents. I became suspicious because Tess seemed to be too perfect in a perfect life. I knew that, sooner or later, something horrible was bound to happen, and I was not let down. When the "black cloud" enters into the story, I wanted to keep reading to find out what was causing this strange thing to happen. So I kept turning the pages to find out. Even though Tess does not have the "black cloud" diagnosed in the beginning, I saw that this story is a love story where Tess explores her feelings and searches for true love. With several elements of a psychological thriller in the plot to keep the mystery moving forward, I could feel that Tess was confused about her dreams, suddenly being woken up by them. She began to consider a man she hardly knew. Tess has many choices to make, but some situations are beyond her control. She struggles with anxiety, lust, anger, and the meaning of life in college. Sex scenes are tender and explicit. One rape scene feels aggressive, which could be an eye-opener for ignorant girls. The ending has more descriptive sexual acts and a classic hunt down. I liked how genetics eventually played a big part in the story. A human-machine philosophy and military intelligence weave into the story. I had to find out what was going to happen to Tess, her love life, and her adorable Gem. For ages 18 and up.<br /><br />Jalpa Williby presents a story using excellent structure and pacing. She unfolds the story intelligently, with detail and affection. Williby knows how to build suspension and keep the reader engaged. She brought the loose ends together for a creative surprise ending.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9372334501357890486" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_706975434" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/706975434" />
    <a title="Bobbie Grob" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7541065-bobbie-grob"><img alt="Bobbie Grob" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1340228101p2/7541065.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/706975434?book_show_action=true">Aug 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bobbie Grob" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bobbie Grob" href="/user/show/7541065-bobbie-grob">Bobbie Grob</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer706975434" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12278810461487209796">Tessnia Sanoby may come off as just your average high school girl as Chaysing Dreams by Jalpa Williby gets going, but it soon becomes clear that there is far more going on inside of Tess than even she knows. As she excels through high school in both athletic and academic achievement and then moves on to college, bits and pieces of the mystery unravel, which kept me highly entertained. There have been quite a few YA fantasy novels to hit the shelves in the last several years, and I’ll admit to op</span>
  <span id="freeText12278810461487209796" style="display:none">Tessnia Sanoby may come off as just your average high school girl as Chaysing Dreams by Jalpa Williby gets going, but it soon becomes clear that there is far more going on inside of Tess than even she knows. As she excels through high school in both athletic and academic achievement and then moves on to college, bits and pieces of the mystery unravel, which kept me highly entertained. There have been quite a few YA fantasy novels to hit the shelves in the last several years, and I’ll admit to opening this one with a bit of a jaded mind. I had hopes that Ms. Williby had brought something new to the genre, but they were not high. As I slowly got sucked into Tess’s life and the life of her friends, her family, and even her dog, I was very pleasantly surprised. This book is familiar enough to be an easy read, and different enough that it kept me guessing. <br /><br />Page one of Chaysing Dreams by Jalpa Williby dropped me straight into a nightmare. The shock of that was a nice entry into Tessnia Sanoby’s world. The only problem Tess has with having an extraordinary life is that she has no clue that her life is anything but slightly-better-than average, even when it is obvious that most everyone around her is in on the secret. The juxtaposition of the incredible with the every day is beautifully done; Ms. Williby definitely knows her stuff. Intrigue? Definitely. Mystery? More than I expected. Just another tweaked version of vampires, werewolves, and dragons? Absolutely not. I thoroughly enjoyed this book, and will be waiting impatiently for the next installment. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12278810461487209796" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_916620843" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/916620843" />
    <a title="Marisa Oldham" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15039221-marisa-oldham"><img alt="Marisa Oldham" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1590268680p2/15039221.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/916620843?book_show_action=true">Apr 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Marisa Oldham" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Marisa Oldham" href="/user/show/15039221-marisa-oldham">Marisa Oldham</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer916620843" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1456627924908871730">Right off the bat, Chaysing Dreams has your wheels turning. The beginning of the book sets the tone for what is a roller coaster ride of a book. I found the story to be engaging and exciting. The beautiful cover and the clever title were what initially attracted me to this book, but the book blurb is what had me practically salivating to read it, the first few pages hooked me, and the following pages kept me turning them.<br/><br/>Although Tessnia is pretty much perfect in every way, I found the emotional</span>
  <span id="freeText1456627924908871730" style="display:none">Right off the bat, Chaysing Dreams has your wheels turning. The beginning of the book sets the tone for what is a roller coaster ride of a book. I found the story to be engaging and exciting. The beautiful cover and the clever title were what initially attracted me to this book, but the book blurb is what had me practically salivating to read it, the first few pages hooked me, and the following pages kept me turning them.<br /><br />Although Tessnia is pretty much perfect in every way, I found the emotional side of this character very easy to relate to. I was on the edge of my seat during some of the scenes and trying so hard to figure out what was going on in others.<br /><br />I loved the author's writing, including the rarely used, in-the-moment, first person, present tense style. I admire the author for having the courage to write a little different from the norm for this genre and she pulled it off very well.<br /><br />The growth of our main character, Tess, is also something that I really enjoyed about this book. We get to see her grow from a teenager into her young adult years. The challenges she faces, although this is a "paranormal" book, are real and really do tug at your emotions. There were moments in this book where I laughed, moments when I cried, and moments where I thought my heart would beat out of my chest.<br />The romantic scenes were some of my favorite in the book because there was so much tension and love involved.<br /><br />I am very excited to read the second book by Williby. I'm looking forward to unraveling the mysteries of this well written story.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1456627924908871730" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_993972443" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/993972443" />
    <a title="Lita Burke" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7119160-lita-burke"><img alt="Lita Burke" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442615022p2/7119160.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/993972443?book_show_action=true">Jul 12, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lita Burke" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lita Burke" href="/user/show/7119160-lita-burke">Lita Burke</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer993972443" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3344864089951206033">Chaysing Dreams by Jalpa Williby is a YA romance about a teenage girl named Tess and her journey to find the meaning of disturbing dreams.<br/><br/>On the outside, Tess lives a charmed life. She is an accomplished athlete. Her schoolwork is effortless perfection. Her super-smart and loving parents give Tess a home filled with luxury. Best of all, she has two super-loyal friends. But inside, dreams about a desperate chase in the woods accompanied by a mysterious man have haunted her for years.<br/><br/>Tess shrugs o</span>
  <span id="freeText3344864089951206033" style="display:none">Chaysing Dreams by Jalpa Williby is a YA romance about a teenage girl named Tess and her journey to find the meaning of disturbing dreams.<br /><br />On the outside, Tess lives a charmed life. She is an accomplished athlete. Her schoolwork is effortless perfection. Her super-smart and loving parents give Tess a home filled with luxury. Best of all, she has two super-loyal friends. But inside, dreams about a desperate chase in the woods accompanied by a mysterious man have haunted her for years.<br /><br />Tess shrugs off the bad dreams and lives her lucky life until a handsome young man holds her breathless during a song. A second alluring and mysterious man becomes her track trainer at college, but leaves abruptly and breaks her heart. The third man reveals that all three have been him in disguise. She learns that his fate entwines with Tess’s and culminates in her nightmare becoming a real panic-filled run through the woods.<br /><br />Chaysing Dreams is a well-told first person story about Tess. It brims with descriptions of a teen’s world. Tess has a refreshing emotional maturity that is usually lacking in YA stories. She is intelligent like her parents, and the story balances it with a teenage girl’s descriptions of clothes and makeup. But this is a YA novel after all, so Tess makes some blunders that land her in big trouble.<br /><br />The story’s climax was excellent, as were the romantic scenes. The story gives Tess a yummy boyfriend, and the reoccurring dreams flowed into a satisfactory conclusion. YA fans looking for a sophisticated heroine would enjoy Chaysing Dreams.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3344864089951206033" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('AonrLsQd5JJge2u07Dt7YQ33olQADdIP/aKs5gTMVFBLdj/Ql6f3XBmg1j+K2QtC6IA5rbV4Jp0MjQ7rngTmKg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('K7DuRxvyMatMOWgUjoRGtTS6H04wMBKvZo9TPuNSCadiTzq5SEgiZTXi1Z/oZjaW0c2Et4VF5j2XoPEzeZq73Q==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer11063356453137380080"><a href='https://readersfavorite.com/2014-award-contest-winners.htm' rel='nofollow noopener'><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409711526i/11011975.png' alt='Readers Favorite Winner' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/>*Award winning author: Gold Medal for Chaysing Dreams and Chaysing Memories for Readers' Favorite International Book Award Contest<br/>*Five Star Seal from Readers' Favorite<br/>*IBD Award (Indie Book of the Day)<br/>*Excellence in Authorship Award (Authors' Cave)<br/>*Finalist for Readers' Favorite International Book Awards in Romance/Suspense, General/Romance, Fiction/Chick Lit, Fiction/Military<br/>Jalpa Williby was b</span>
  <span id="freeText11063356453137380080" style="display:none"><a href="https://readersfavorite.com/2014-award-contest-winners.htm" rel="nofollow noopener"><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409711526i/11011975.png" alt="Readers Favorite Winner" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>*Award winning author: Gold Medal for Chaysing Dreams and Chaysing Memories for Readers' Favorite International Book Award Contest<br>*Five Star Seal from Readers' Favorite<br>*IBD Award (Indie Book of the Day)<br>*Excellence in Authorship Award (Authors' Cave)<br>*Finalist for Readers' Favorite International Book Awards in Romance/Suspense, General/Romance, Fiction/Chick Lit, Fiction/Military<br>Jalpa Williby was born in India and immigrated to the United States at the tender age of eight. A voracious reader, Williby’s adolescence was marked by a promising academic career. After graduating with a Bachelors of Science from the University of Illinois, Williby went on to earn Masters in Physical Therapy from Northwestern University. Her passion for helping her patients led her to a specialty in neuroscience, focusing on children and adults with neurological impairments. Juggling her time as a wife, a mother, and working full-time, her love for books never subsided. Since the success of her debut novel, Chaysing Dreams, Williby recently released the sequel, Chaysing Memories. Both novels have done exceptionally well. With both novels being Amazon best sellers, more recently, they both won the Gold Medal in Readers' Favorite International Book Award Contest. Williby is currently working feverishly on her third and final installment of the Chaysing Trilogy as she writes with her heart and soul, her passion flowing through every page. </span>
